posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:This may be the best hotel in Tekes County. A small county with such a high level of service shows that this is a tourist city.
Location: About 5 kilometers from the county. If you come early, you can go to the county to have a look.
Facilities: A new hotel within two years. The room is quite new and large. The humidifier is well received. The bathroom is separated into wet and dry areas.
Service: The front desk staff is very enthusiastic and service-minded. There are staff who help guests with luggage and send them to the room. When checking out, they ask if they are satisfied and have any suggestions. They also give a piece of exquisite soap as a souvenir.
Breakfast: Rich, with freshly cooked noodles and rice noodles, yogurt, fruits, snacks, etc.
Parking: There are plenty of parking spaces. There was a wedding banquet that day and it was the May Day holiday. There were plenty of parking spaces, and there were several parking lots.
Disadvantages: The surrounding area is a little desolate, there are construction sites, no restaurants and convenience stores, and you have to go to the county to eat.
Overall evaluation: Very good. If you go to Kalajun, I recommend staying here.
